                            UPDATE t_bmsupplierlink 
                            SET gender = CASE 
                                WHEN gender = '男' THEN 'Male'
                                WHEN gender = '女' THEN 'Female'

                                ELSE gender END
                            WHERE gender IN (
                                '男', '女'); error:22001: 对于可变字符类型来说，值太长了(5)

Log Entry : 18:54:14 2025年2月23日 

                            UPDATE t_rcjprojectcostfeeids 
                            SET feetype = CASE 

                                WHEN feetype = '在用' Then 'InUse'
                                WHEN feetype = '备用' THEN 'Backup'
                                WHEN feetype = '基准' THEN 'Baseline'

                                WHEN feetype = '采购件' Then 'PurchParts'
                                WHEN feetype = '自制件' THEN 'MadeParts'
                                WHEN feetype = '外协件' THEN 'OutParts'
                                WHEN feetype = '交付件' THEN 'DelivParts'

                                WHEN feetype = '房屋租凭' THEN 'HouseRental'
                                WHEN feetype = '市场营销' THEN 'Marketing'
                                WHEN feetype = '考勤管理' THEN 'AttendanceManagement'
                                WHEN feetype = '招标管理' THEN 'TenderManagement'
                                WHEN feetype = '运营管理' THEN 'OperationManagement'
                                WHEN feetype = '供应商管理' THEN 'SupplierManagement'
                                WHEN feetype = '分包申请' THEN 'SubcontractApplication'
                                WHEN feetype = '费用报销' THEN 'ExpenseReimbursement'
                                WHEN feetype = '设计生产' THEN 'DesignAndProduction'
                                WHEN feetype = '计划审批' THEN 'PlanApproval'
                                WHEN feetype = '招标计划' THEN 'TenderPlan'
                                WHEN feetype = '付款申请' THEN 'PaymentRequest'
                                WHEN feetype = '费用申请' THEN 'ExpenseRequest'
                                WHEN feetype = '签证管理' THEN 'VisaManagement'
                                WHEN feetype = '计划评审' THEN 'PlanReview'
                                WHEN feetype = '发票处理' THEN 'InvoiceProcessing'
                                WHEN feetype = '项目评审' THEN 'ProjectReview'
                                WHEN feetype = '状态评审' THEN 'StatusReview'

                                WHEN feetype = '任务评审' THEN 'TaskReview'
                                WHEN feetype = '出差申请' THEN 'BusinessTripRequest'
                                WHEN feetype = '物料采购' THEN 'MaterialProcurement'
                                WHEN feetype = '物料领用' THEN 'MaterialWithdrawal'
                                WHEN feetype = '文件评审' THEN 'DocumentReview'
                                WHEN feetype = '资产采购' THEN 'AssetProcurement'
                                WHEN feetype = '物料销售' THEN 'MaterialSales'
                                WHEN feetype = '资产领用' THEN 'AssetWithdrawal'
                                WHEN feetype = '物料供货' THEN 'MaterialSupply'
                                WHEN feetype = '投标管理' THEN 'BidManagement'

                                WHEN feetype = '物料生产' THEN 'MaterialProduction'
                                WHEN feetype = '合同评审' THEN 'ContractReview'

                                WHEN feetype = '风险评估' THEN 'RiskAssessment'
